acCreateUser() {
    acPreProcForCreateUser();
    acCreateUserF1();
    acPostProcForCreateUser();
}
acCreateUserF1() {
    on ($otherUserName == "anonymous") {
        msiCreateUser():::msiRollback();
        msiCommit();
    }
acCreateUserF1() {
    msiCreateUser():::msiRollback();
    acCreateDefaultCollections():::msiRollback();
    msiAddUserToGroup("public"):::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}
acVacuum(*arg1) {
    delayExec(*arg1," msiVacuum;","");
}
acCreateDefaultCollections() {
    acCreateUserZoneCollections();
}
acCreateUserZoneCollections() {
    acCreateCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/home",$otherUserName);
    acCreateCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/trash/home",$otherUserName);
}
acCreateCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl) {
    msiCreateCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl);
}
acDeleteUser() {
    acPreProcForDeleteUser();
    acDeleteUserF1();
    acPostProcForDeleteUser();
}
acDeleteUserF1() {
    acDeleteDefaultCollections():::msiRollback();
    msiDeleteUser():::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}
acDeleteDefaultCollections() {
    acDeleteUserZoneCollections();
}
acDeleteUserZoneCollections() {
    acDeleteCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/home",$otherUserName);
    acDeleteCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/trash/home",$otherUserName);
}
acDeleteCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl) {
    msiDeleteCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl);
}
acRenameLocalZone(*oldZone,*newZone) {
    msiRenameCollection("/" ++ str(*oldZone) ++ "",*newZone):::msiRollback();
    msiRenameLocalZone(*oldZone,*newZone):::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}

acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {

        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }

        cut();
    }

    on (*Action == "list") {

        cut();
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    on ((*Condition == "null") %% (*Condition == "")) {
        msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
        acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\'",*List);
        foreach (*List) {
            msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
            writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
        }
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
    acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\' AND " ++ str(*Condition) ++ "",*List);
    foreach (*List) {
        msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
        writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
    }
}
acConvertToInt(*R) {
    *A = $sysUidClient;
    $sysUidClient = *R;
    *K = $sysUidClient;
    *R = *K;
    $sysUidClient = *A;
}

acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on ((*Action == "replicate") %% (*Action == "trim") %% (*Action == "chksum") %% (*Action == "copy") %% (*Action == "remove")) {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "chksumRescLoc") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, RESC_LOC",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "list") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, DATA_RESC_NAME, DATA_REPL_NUM, DATA_SIZE",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    on ((*Condition == "null") %% (*Condition == "")) {
        msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
        acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\'",*List);
        foreach (*List) {
            msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
            writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
        }
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
    acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\' AND " ++ str(*Condition) ++ "",*List);
    foreach (*List) {
        msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
        writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
    }
}
acConvertToInt(*R) {
    *A = $sysUidClient;
    $sysUidClient = *R;
    *K = $sysUidClient;
    *R = *K;
    $sysUidClient = *A;
}
publicGroupPermissions() {
    on ($objPath like "/test1/home/test1/pub/\*") {
        msiWriteRodsLog("--- INSIDE publicGroupPermissions ---",*Status);

acCreateUser() {
    acPreProcForCreateUser();
    acCreateUserF1();
    acPostProcForCreateUser();
}
acCreateUserF1() {
    on ($otherUserName == "anonymous") {
        msiCreateUser():::msiRollback();
        msiCommit();
    }
acCreateUserF1() {
    msiCreateUser():::msiRollback();
    acCreateDefaultCollections():::msiRollback();
    msiAddUserToGroup("public"):::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}
acVacuum(*arg1) {
    delayExec(*arg1," msiVacuum;","");
}
acCreateDefaultCollections() {
    acCreateUserZoneCollections();
}
acCreateUserZoneCollections() {
    acCreateCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/home",$otherUserName);
    acCreateCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/trash/home",$otherUserName);
}
acCreateCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl) {
    msiCreateCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl);
}
acDeleteUser() {
    acPreProcForDeleteUser();
    acDeleteUserF1();
    acPostProcForDeleteUser();
}
acDeleteUserF1() {
    acDeleteDefaultCollections():::msiRollback();
    msiDeleteUser():::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}
acDeleteDefaultCollections() {
    acDeleteUserZoneCollections();
}
acDeleteUserZoneCollections() {
    acDeleteCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/home",$otherUserName);
    acDeleteCollByAdmin("/" ++ $rodsZoneProxy ++ "/trash/home",$otherUserName);
}
acDeleteCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl) {
    msiDeleteCollByAdmin(*parColl,*childColl);
}
acRenameLocalZone(*oldZone,*newZone) {
    msiRenameCollection("/" ++ str(*oldZone) ++ "",*newZone):::msiRollback();
    msiRenameLocalZone(*oldZone,*newZone):::msiRollback();
    msiCommit();
}

    msiCommit();

acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on ((*Action == "replicate") %% (*Action == "trim") %% (*Action == "chksum") %% (*Action == "copy") %% (*Action == "remove")) {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "chksumRescLoc") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, RESC_LOC",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "list") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, DATA_RESC_NAME, DATA_REPL_NUM, DATA_SIZE",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    on ((*Condition == "null") %% (*Condition == "")) {
        msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
        acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\'",*List);
        foreach (*List) {
            msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
            writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
        }
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
    acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\' AND " ++ str(*Condition) ++ "",*List);
    foreach (*List) {
        msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
        writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
    }
}
acConvertToInt(*R) {
    *A = $sysUidClient;
    $sysUidClient = *R;
    *K = $sysUidClient;
    *R = *K;
    $sysUidClient = *A;
}

acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on ((*Action == "replicate") %% (*Action == "trim") %% (*Action == "chksum") %% (*Action == "copy") %% (*Action == "remove")) {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "chksumRescLoc") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, RESC_LOC",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "list") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, DATA_RESC_NAME, DATA_REPL_NUM, DATA_SIZE",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    on ((*Condition == "null") %% (*Condition == "")) {
        msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
        acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\'",*List);
        foreach (*List) {
            msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
            writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
        }
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
    acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\' AND " ++ str(*Condition) ++ "",*List);
    foreach (*List) {
        msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
        writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
    }
}
acConvertToInt(*R) {
    *A = $sysUidClient;
    $sysUidClient = *R;
    *K = $sysUidClient;
    *R = *K;
    $sysUidClient = *A;
}

acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on ((*Action == "replicate") %% (*Action == "trim") %% (*Action == "chksum") %% (*Action == "copy") %% (*Action == "remove")) {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "chksumRescLoc") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, RESC_LOC",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acGetIcatResults(*Action,*Condition,*GenQOut) {
    on (*Action == "list") {
        msiMakeQuery("DATA_NAME, COLL_NAME, DATA_RESC_NAME, DATA_REPL_NUM, DATA_SIZE",*Condition,*Query);
        msiExecStrCondQuery(*Query,*GenQOut);
        cut();
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    on ((*Condition == "null") %% (*Condition == "")) {
        msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
        acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\'",*List);
        foreach (*List) {
            msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
            msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
            writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
        }
    }
acPurgeFiles(*Condition) {
    msiGetIcatTime(*Time,"unix");
    acGetIcatResults("remove","DATA_EXPIRY < \'" ++ str(*Time) ++ "\' AND " ++ str(*Condition) ++ "",*List);
    foreach (*List) {
        msiDataObjUnlink(*List,*Status);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"DATA_NAME",*D);
        msiGetValByKey(*List,"COLL_NAME",*E);
        writeLine("stdout","Purged File " ++ str(*E) ++ "/" ++ str(*D) ++ " at " ++ str(*Time) ++ "");
    }
}
acConvertToInt(*R) {
    *A = $sysUidClient;
    $sysUidClient = *R;
    *K = $sysUidClient;
    *R = *K;
    $sysUidClient = *A;
